<text>After searching endlessly for a good dumpling place to replace my now-closed goto one, I finally decided to try Full House Dumpling. The wait can be a bit long, as it is usually packed for the weekends. The dumplings are well worth the wait however. They're served in a traditional fashion and comes fresh and steaming hot. I recommend the pork dumplings and the pork with crab. Every dumpling is made just right, stuffed with juicy meat and a bit of broth inside. The thin onion pancakes are also well made, being fried just the right amount. The beef rolls are a bit lackluster with an overpowering beef taste, but I can see how some may enjoy it. Their seafood warm pot compliments the other dishes well, allowing you to reset your taste buds. It is a huge pot however, so I recommend you only ordering it if you have a party of 4 or more. They do offer to-go containers if you don't finish though. Overall, this place is definitely worth a try.<//text>< rate>
4</rate>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
Great restaurant. They're known for their soup dumplings and that was certainly excellent. I'm not usually a fan of soup dumplings with crab but the ones here reminded me of China so much that I actually prefer them here. The rest of the dumplings were less superb. Pork and chive potstickers for instance were average, skin too loose and flimsy, bottom crust not well developed. I had the pork belly with buns dish which was pretty good. Really I'd stick with the soup dumplings and maybe their hotpot style dishes.<//text>

<pics>None<//pics><text>Grand opening sign hanging outside! I'm not sure when it actually opened, but it was not crowded when we came this weekend! The restaurant is very clean and feels very open, and modern (great use of wood decor)- quite different from most Asian places. Service was great as well.

To be honest, food was not too bad, but yes, there are better dumplings elsewhere in Fremont. Our party ordered:
+Shrimp xlb - not bad, though after you drink the soup inside, it tasted a tad dry
+ Pork xlb - good amount of soup inside with lots of flavor, and the wrap wasn't too thick. I would recommend getting this
+ Pork Dumplings - Pretty good and very soupy! I liked this a lot.
+ Shrimp Fried Rice - Average, not much worth raving about
+Spare Ribs  - Average
+Green Onion Pancake - Very unique in the sense that the order is SUPER small (think a normal size pork bun or something, and squash it down to flatten, and cut into 6 pieces), and the filling is (heavy)black pepper with green onions . If you like black pepper, you will enjoy this.
+Red bean paste sesame pancake (dessert)- This was very yummy! I think I ate 3 pieces? Nice and thin, and tasty.

Come by and give it a try yourself! I love that Fremont is now having so many dumpling options!<//text>< gmap_id>

< review>
I had high expectations because of the high ratings and photos. I give 4 stars for their friendly, awesome service, but I honestly threw away both my teas because they were too sweet. I had requested minimal sweetness, but both were super sweet. I got the lychee cucumber tea and strawberry daiquiri.

I am used to boba shops that give options for great tasting tea without all the sugar, but Teaspoon was disappointing in that regard. I wanted to try Taro with only a slight sweetness, but they didn't offer that option.

I went to Teabo and ordered a matcha tea with zero sweetness, and I was pleasantly surprised that they gave me a matcha tea with exactly zero sweetness. Awesome. I hope Teaspoon can find ways to offer great tea with better options for adjusting sweetness.<//review>

<name>Talal P<//name><Pictures>None</Pictures><Rating>1< /Rating>< review>
If you are on a fixed income please do yourself a favor and stay away from this place.

My mother has been down on her luck lately and moved out of her apartment, she needed a storage space so we moved her belongings here into a 10x20 priced at $224. plus the $9.00 insurance when they were owned by StorQuest. I've been paying the bulk of it to take some of the stress off of her.

As soon as ExtraSpace took over they raised the rent. It was only $10 and my insurance went up $1, so I could look passed that. It's been a few months and starting Jan. 01 2015 they are raising the rent $33 bringing my total to 267.00.

I don't appreciate being nickle and dimed. I've honored my rent commitment, on time, every month with no hassle but I refuse to be screwed over.

I would be more understanding if they raised it at the beginning of a new lease but attempting to slide it in the middle and expect us to take it lying down is despicable.

I will being taking my business elsewhere</review>
